The Muskie Malaise

" e.pages = ["

Ed Muskie’s term would hardly be stable. Lee Atwater, Karl Rove, Paul Weyrich - all of them were on the outs with the party establishment thanks to you, and all of them latched onto an obscure two-term governor of Maryland nominally aligned with the infant Romneyites but far more conservative in practice, Spiro Agnew. Agnew’s fifty-state organization paid dividends with surprise victory after victory, and his momentum quickly gathered as legions of suburbanites saw the normalcy they craved embodied in him.
